msg:The overall evaluation is: cheap, not worthy of the name.

This review is based on the experience of a luxury hotel. If this hotel is really positioned as an express hotel, then there is nothing to say.

As an IHG hotel, are you not afraid to smash IHG's signature? For the price of seven or eight hundred and one night, staying in a fast hotel feels cheap. There is no Crowne Plaza experience in other cities. There is no harm if there is no comparison. The previous stay IHG was at Nanjing Yangtze River Boat. The overall experience is not better than Ningbo Kaizhou. Even before, I have stayed in Crowne Plaza in third- and fourth-tier cities, and the experience is much better than Ningbo Kaizhou.

1 Service
There is nothing bad about the service. However, there is a complaint that the slipper frame has written to provide shoe shine service, as shown in Figure 1. I have also enjoyed this kind of service in other IHG hotels before (although only the waiter wiped it with liquid shoe polish). But when I called the service center, my younger brother said, "We don't have this service here. Send two shoeshine cloths?". First of all, you don't provide this service, why do you want to put this brand? Second, the shoe polishing cloth, shouldn't it be there? As IHG's "luxury" hotels, don't they generally have shoe polishes and round shoe polishes?

2 Hardware
Outdated facilities. I checked it later and found out that it was renovated in 2012. You can see the wall in Figure 2 below, and the shower head in the bathroom in Figure 3 (the conditioner is not there, which is worse than the Express Hotel). One more thing, the water coming out of the shower head is like a goddess's flowers. The carpet is also uneven. It is estimated that the ground itself is not level, so a carpet is used to cover it.

3 Software aspects

The toilet paper towel is a single-layer paper towel, as shown in Figure 4. It is a real and fast hotel feel. Using better paper will not increase the cost.

Toiletries are also a sense of a fast hotel, as shown in Figure 5. Although it is said that in response to the national call (but more of the hotel wants to reduce costs), the hotel does not provide combs, cotton swabs, shower caps and other disposable items, but it is a bit advanced. Doesn't it feel good? Using a plastic box with two cheap toothbrushes is not so shabby in the Express Hotel.

In addition, the equipment in question needs to be maintained in advance. The so-called uninterruptible power socket is broken, as shown in Figure 5. I charged the computer on it at night and took a rest. I woke up in the morning and found that there was no charging at all, so I hurriedly changed the socket and charged it for a while. Why is the socket problem found? It was because the 220v socket in the bathroom was also broken. The hair dryer didn't work in the morning, so I plugged it into this socket and found that the socket was dead.

Also, when I was sleeping, the pillow smelled of smoke. Fortunately, there were four pillows. I chose a pillow that was not too smelly and slept all night.

There are other slots, not listed one by one. For example, if the window is dirty, see Figure 6. For example, the swivel chair is old and unbearable. For example, the remote control buttons are difficult to press. It’s bad, as shown in Figure 7. For another example, if you build a delivery robot (shoe polishing cloth is delivered by the robot), what users want is a real accommodation experience. What is the use of a robot delivery gimmick? ?

Users staying in Crowne Plaza, IHG series hotels, the picture shows a good sense of experience, Crowne Plaza Ningbo Kaizhou, the name does not fit the truth.

msg:5分好評是給服務的。前台接待是實習生，但是也是彬彬有禮，態度熱情。我們是臨時定的酒店，路上就有電話過來，詢問達到時間和房間是否要求無煙，還為我們爭取了免費早餐。打電話過來的Nancy專業有禮，離店第二天因為賬單的問題聯繫她，也非常迅速的幫忙查詢和解決。從服務來説，不愧是老牌商務五星酒店。
